function setProductModal()
{
	$('a[rel*=facebox]').facebox({
		loadingImage : '/data/daiso_data/templet/daiso/images/loading.gif',
		closeImage   : '/data/daiso_data/templet/daiso/images/close_btn01.gif'
	});

}

$(document).ready(function(){
	$(".slide_banner_box").find(".s_l_b").hide();
	$(".slide_banner_box").hover(
		function(){
			$(this).find(".s_l_b").fadeIn();
		},
		function(){
			$(this).find(".s_l_b").fadeOut("fast");
	});
});

</script>

<script type="text/javascript">
	$(document).ready(function(){
		
		$('#app_install').submit(function(){
			if($('input[name="tel_2"]').val() == ""){
				alert('핸드폰번호를 입력해주세요');
				$(this).focus();
				return false;
			}

			if($('input[name="tel_3"]').val() == ""){
				alert('핸드폰번호를 입력해주세요');
				$(this).focus();
				return false;
			}

			var valuesToSubmit = $(this).serialize();
			$.ajax({
				url: $(this).attr('action'), 
				data: valuesToSubmit,
				dataType: "html" 
			}).success(function(data){
				
					alert(data);
					//location.reload();
			});
			return false; 

		});

		//$("span").removeClass("HelpCloud-mains");
		$(".go_admin").hide();
		$(".md-after-content").find("br").remove();
		

		mainBannerAction(0);
		var mainBanner = setInterval('mainBannerAction(null)', 3000);
		$('.mainBannerArea ,.banner_cate li a').hover(function()	{
			clearInterval(mainBanner);
		}, function()
		{
			mainBanner = setInterval('mainBannerAction(null)', 3000);
		});

		$(".banner_cate li").mouseover(function(){
			mainBannerAction($(this).index())
		});
	});
	
	function mainBannerAction(index){
		var area = $('.mainBannerArea');
		var cnt = area.find("a").length;
		var now_obj = $('.mainBannerArea a:visible');
		now_obj.hide();
		
		if(index!=null){
			area.find("a").eq(index).show();
		}else{
			index = area.find("a").index(now_obj)+1;

			if(cnt > index){
				now_obj.next("a").show();
			}else{
				index=0;
				area.find("a:first").show();
			}
		}

		$(".banner_cate li").eq(index).addClass("on");
		$(".banner_cate li").eq(index).siblings().removeClass("on");

		$(".banner_cate li").eq(index).siblings().find("img").each(function(){
			$(this).attr("src",$(this).attr("outImg"));
		})
		var now_img_obj = $(".banner_cate li").eq(index).find("img");
		now_img_obj.attr("src",now_img_obj.attr("overImg"));
	}

	$(".custuMselect").selectbox();	

	$(".close_top").click(function(){
		$(".header_top").slideUp("fast");
		
	});

	$(".my_shopping").click(function(){
		$(".my_shopping_info").slideToggle("fast");
	});
	
	
</script>

<script type="text/javascript"> 


$(".total_cate_show").click(function(){
	$(this).parent().parent().next(".total_cate_box").slideToggle("fast");
});

$("select[name^=cid]").selectbox();

$(".custom_select").selectbox();

$("select[name=main_search]").selectbox();

/* 자동완성시 검색영역 노출되므로 주석처리 2014-07-09 JBG
$("#search_texts").focus(function(){
	$(".relation_search").show();
});

$(".relation_search").blur(function(){
	$(".relation_search").hide();
});
*/

$("#search-scroll-search").focus(function(){
	if ($(this).css("font-weight","normal"))
	{
		$(this).val("");
		$(this).css("font-weight","bold")
	}
	
});

$(".btn_close").click(function(){
	$(".relation_search").hide();
});

$(".btn_over02 a").hover(function(){
	if($(this).find("img").attr("src").substring($(this).find("img").attr("src").length-7)!="_on.png"){
		$(this).find("img").attr("src",$(this).find("img").attr("src").replace(".png","_on.png"));
		$(this).next("span").show();
	}
	else{
		$(this).find("img").attr("src",$(this).find("img").attr("src").replace("_on.png",".png"));
		$(this).next('span').hide();
	}
});

function headerTopRightBtnReset(){
	$(".toggle_img").each(function(){
		$(this).find("img").attr("src",$(this).find("img").attr("src").replace("_on.gif",".gif"));
		$(this).parent().find("dd").hide();
	});

}
$(".toggle_img").click(function(){
	if($(this).find("img").attr("src").substring($(this).find("img").attr("src").length-7)!="_on.gif"){
		headerTopRightBtnReset();
		$(this).find("img").attr("src",$(this).find("img").attr("src").replace(".gif","_on.gif"));
		$(this).parent().find("dd").show();
	}
	else{
		$(this).find("img").attr("src",$(this).find("img").attr("src").replace("_on.gif",".gif"));
		$(this).parent().find("dd").hide();
	}
});

/* Search Field Validation */
	$(function(){
		if ( $('.field-search').val() == '' ) {
			$('.field-search').val($('.field-search').attr('data'));
		}
		
		$('.field-search').on({
			focusin: function(){
				var randomText = $(this).attr('data');
				var currentText = $(this).val();
				if ( randomText == currentText ) {
					$(this).val('');
				}
			},
			focusout: function(){
				var randomText = $(this).attr('data');
				var currentText = $(this).val();
				if ( currentText == '' ) {
					$(this).val(randomText);
				}
			}
		});
	});
/* Search Field Validation */

</script>

<script type="text/javascript">
var menuMoveTime =30,
	menuCloseTime = 50,
	menuTimer,
	closeTimer,
	menuObj;
	$(".c_menu01").each(function() {
		$(this).mouseover(function() {
			$(".left_category").addClass("on");
			$(".left_cate_bg_bottom").addClass("on");
			clearTimeout(closeTimer);
			menuObj = $(this);
			menuTimer = setTimeout(function () {
				$(".c_menu01").removeClass("on");
				$(".c_menu01").find(".second_depth").hide();
		        menuObj.addClass("on");
				menuObj.find(".second_depth").show();
		    }, menuMoveTime);
		});
		$(this).mouseout(function() {
			clearTimeout(menuTimer);
		});
	});
	$(".left_category").mouseout(function(){
		$(".left_category").removeClass("on");
		closeTimer = setTimeout(function(){		             
			$(".left_cate_bg_bottom").removeClass("on");
            $(".c_menu01").removeClass("on");
			$(".c_menu01").find(".second_depth").hide();
		},menuCloseTime); 
	});
	
	$(".second_depth_banner").find(".btn_over").hide();
	$(".second_depth_banner").hover(
		function(){
			$(this).find(".btn_over").fadeIn();
		},
		function(){
			$(this).find(".btn_over").fadeOut("fast");
		});


</script>

			<div class='right_wrap'>

					<div class="main_unbg"><script>
	var history2 = new Array(); // history 로 변수명을 사용할 경우 파폭에서 setting a property that has only a getter 에러 발생 kbk


	function Today_Tmp(hist){
	var mstring_ = "";
	mstring_ += "	<li style='margin-bottom:6px;'>";
	mstring_ += "		<a href='/shop/goods_view.php?cid="+hist[1]+"&id="+hist[0]+"'><img src='"+hist[3]+"' border=0 onerror=\"$(this).hide();\" width='58' height='58' align=absmiddle style='border:1px solid #e6e6e6;'> </a>";
	mstring_ += "	</li>";

	return mstring_;
	}

	var view_size = 3;
	var num_ = Math.ceil(history2.length/view_size);
	var total_num_ = history2.length;
	var total_pnum_ = Math.ceil(history2.length/view_size);

	function today_history(con_num){
		var m_mstring = "";
		var mstring = "";
		if(num_==0) {
			$("#today_history_page_num").html("0");
			$("#today_history_total_num").html("0");
			$("#today_products").html("");
		} else {
			if(con_num!="") {
				var test_num_=num_ + con_num;
				//alert(test_num_);
				if(test_num_ > total_pnum_){
					alert('더이상 품목이 없습니다.');
					return;
				}

				//if(num_ < view_size-1){
				if(test_num_==0){
					alert('더이상 품목이 없습니다.');
					return;
				}
				num_ = num_ + con_num;
			}
			if(num_>1) {
				var roof_num=view_size;
			} else {
				if(total_num_%view_size==0 && total_num_>0) var roof_num=view_size;
				else var roof_num=total_num_%view_size;
			}
			var roof_string="";
			for(i=0;i<roof_num;i++){
				var start_num=(total_num_ - ((total_pnum_ - num_)*view_size) -i)-1;
				roof_string+=Today_Tmp(history2[start_num]);
			}
			$("#today_history_page_num").html(total_pnum_ - (num_ - 1));
			$("#today_history_total_num").html(total_pnum_);
			$("#today_products").html(roof_string);
		}
	}
	
	right_menu_cart_loding=false;
	right_menu_coupon_loding=false;
	right_menu_recent_loding=false;

	$(document).ready(function(){
		$('.right_over_menu').mouseover(function(){

			if($(this).attr("class").indexOf("cart") > 0){
				if(!right_menu_cart_loding){
					right_menu_control("cart","loding");
					right_menu_cart_loding=true;
				}
			}else if($(this).attr("class").indexOf("coupon") > 0){
				if(!right_menu_coupon_loding){
					right_menu_control("coupon","loding");
					right_menu_coupon_loding=true;
				}
			}else if($(this).attr("class").indexOf("recent") > 0){
				if(!right_menu_recent_loding){
					right_menu_control("recent","loding");
					right_menu_recent_loding=true;
				}
			}

			var img_state_type2 = $(this).find('.right_goods_img').attr('src').indexOf('ov');
			var src = $(this).find('.right_goods_img').attr('src').replace('.gif','_ov.gif');
			
			if (img_state_type2 <= 0)
			{
				$(this).find('.right_goods_img').attr('src',src);
				$(this).find('.right_over_wrap').show();
				$(this).find('.right_goods_img').css({'z-index':'23'});
			}

		}).mouseleave(function(){
			var src2 = $(this).find('.right_goods_img').attr('src').replace('_ov.gif','.gif');
			$(this).find('.right_goods_img').attr('src',src2)
			$(this).find('.right_over_wrap').hide();
			$(this).find('.right_goods_img').css({'z-index':'20'});
		})

			$('.cart_goods_wrap li').each(function(){
				var inx_n = ($('.cart_goods_wrap li').index($(this))+1)%2;
				if (inx_n == 0)
				{
					$(this).css({'margin-left':'23px'});
				}
			});

		$('.pop_close_class').click(function(){
			$(".right_over_menu").trigger("mouseleave");
		});

		$(window).scroll(function(){
			var scroll_Now = $(window).scrollTop();
			var scroll_header = $('#header').height();
			if (scroll_header <= scroll_Now)
			{
				$('.wing_banners').addClass('Q_menu_position_type1').removeClass('Q_menu_position_type2');
			}else {
				$('.wing_banners').addClass('Q_menu_position_type2').removeClass('Q_menu_position_type1');
			}
		});

		today_history("");
		
	});

	
	///////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////////// Hong 2014-06-25


	function right_menu_control(ptype,act,ix){
		var right_cart_max = 4;
		var right_coupon_max = 5;
		var right_recent_max = 8;
		var max = 4;

		if(act=="delete"||act=="delete_all"){
			if(parseInt($("#right_"+ptype+"_total_num").text())!=0){
				if(!confirm('정말 삭제하시겠습니까?')){
					return false;
				}
			}else{
				alert('삭제할 상품이 없습니다.');
				return false;
			}

		}

		total_page = parseInt($("#right_"+ptype+"_total_num").text());
		now_page = parseInt($("#right_"+ptype+"_page_num").text());

		if(act=="next"){
			act="select_data";
			page = now_page+1;
			if(page > total_page){
				page=1;
			}
		}else if(act=="previous"){
			act="select_data";
			page = now_page-1;
			if(page==0){
				page = total_page;
			}
		}else if(act=="loding"){
			act="select_data";
			page=1;
		}else{
			page=now_page;
		}
		
		if(ptype=="cart"){
			max = right_cart_max;
		}else if(ptype=="coupon"){
			max = right_coupon_max;
		}else if(ptype=="recent"){
			max = right_recent_max;
		}

		if(!(page==1&&total_page==1) || act!="select_data"){
			
			dataString = {"ptype":ptype,"act":act,"page":page,"max":max,"ix":ix};

			$.ajax({ 
				type: 'POST',
				data: dataString,  
				url: '/include/right_menu_slides.php',
				dataType: 'json', 
				async: false, 
				beforeSend: function(){

				},
				error: function(datas){
					//alert("error");
				},
				success: function(datas){ 
					//alert(datas);
					if(ptype=="cart"){
						right_cart_data_set(datas);
					}else if(ptype=="coupon"){
						right_coupon_data_set(datas);
					}else if(ptype=="recent"){
						right_recent_data_set(datas);
					}
				}
			});
		}
	}

	function right_cart_data_set(datas){
		if(datas !="N"){
			$(".cart_info_visible[view=is]").show();
			$(".cart_info_visible[view=no]").hide();
			$("#right_cart_total_num").text(datas.total_page);
			$("#right_cart_page_num").text(datas.page);

			$("#right_cart_total_product_price").text(datas.total_product_price);
			$("#right_cart_total_delivery_price").text(datas.total_delivery_price);
			$("#right_cart_total_price").text(datas.total_price);
			
			$(".cart_info_visible[view=is] .cart_goods_wrap li").remove();
			var str = "";
			$(datas.product).each(function(i,pinfo){
				str += '	<li>';
				str += '		<dl>';
				str += '			<dt>';
				str += '				<a href="/shop/goods_view.php?id='+pinfo.id+'"><img src="'+pinfo.img+'" alt="" width="85" height="85" /></a>';
				str += '				<span><img src="/data/daiso_data/templet/daiso/images/korea/common/right_type_close2.gif" alt="close2" onclick="right_menu_control(\'cart\',\'delete\','+pinfo.cart_ix+');" /></span>';
				str += '			</dt>';
				str += '			<dd>';
				str += '				<strong>'+pinfo.price+'</strong>원';
				str += '			</dd>';
				str += '		</dl>';
				str += '	</li>';
			});

			$(".cart_info_visible[view=is] .cart_goods_wrap").append(str);
			$(".cart_goods_wrap").find("li:odd").css("margin-left","23px");
		}else{
			$(".cart_info_visible[view=is]").hide();
			$(".cart_info_visible[view=no]").show();
			$("#right_cart_total_product_price").text(0);
			$("#right_cart_total_delivery_price").text(0);
			$("#right_cart_total_price").text(0);
		}
	}

	function right_coupon_data_set(datas){
		if(datas =="N"){
			$(".coupon_info_visible[view=login]").hide();
			$(".coupon_info_visible[view=is]").hide();
			$(".coupon_info_visible[view=no]").show();
		}else if(datas =="login"){
			$(".coupon_info_visible[view=login]").show();
			$(".coupon_info_visible[view=is]").hide();
			$(".coupon_info_visible[view=no]").hide();
		}else{
			$("#right_coupon_total_cnt").text(datas.total_cnt);
			$("#right_coupon_total_num").text(datas.total_page);
			$("#right_coupon_page_num").text(datas.page);

			$(".coupon_info_visible[view=login]").hide();
			$(".coupon_info_visible[view=is]").show();
			$(".coupon_info_visible[view=no]").hide();

			$(".coupon_info_visible[view=is] .coupon_list dl").remove();
			var str = "";
			$(datas.coupon).each(function(i,cinfo){
				str += '	<dl>';
				str += '		<dt>';
				str += '			<img src="'+cinfo.img+'" alt="" width="90" height="48" />';
				str += '		</dt>';
				str += '		<dd>';
				str += '			<ul>';
				str += '				<li style="color:#2a2a2a; margin:9px 0px 8px;">';
				str += '					'+cinfo.title+'할인';
				str += '				</li>';
				str += '				<li>';
				str += '					['+cinfo.desc+']';
				str += '				</li>';
				str += '			</ul>';
				str += '		</dd>';
				str += '	</dl>';
			});
			$(".coupon_info_visible[view=is] .coupon_list").append(str);
		}
	}

	function right_recent_data_set(datas){
		// if(datas.exist_count > 0 || datas.add_count > 0){
			// alert('찜하기 ' + datas.add_count + ' 개의 상품이 정상적으로 등록 되었습니다.\n이미 등록된 상품이 ' + datas.exist_count + ' 개 입니다.');
		// }
		//console.log(datas);
		if ( datas.exist_count > 0 && datas.add_count > 0 ) {
			alert(datas.add_count + '개의 상품이 찜하기에 등록되었습니다.\n총 찜하기 등록하신 상품은 ' + datas.exist_count + ' 개 입니다.');
		} else if ( datas.add_count != null && datas.exist_count != null ) {
			alert('이미 찜하신 상품입니다.\n총 찜하기 등록하신 상품은 ' + datas.exist_count + ' 개 입니다.');
		}

		if(datas =="N"){
			$(".recent_info_visible[view=is]").hide();
			$(".recent_info_visible[view=no]").show();
			$(".recent_info_visible[view=login]").hide();
		}else if(datas =="login"){
			$(".recent_info_visible[view=is]").hide();
			$(".recent_info_visible[view=no]").hide();
			$(".recent_info_visible[view=login]").show();
		}else{
			$(".recent_info_visible[view=is]").show();
			$(".recent_info_visible[view=no]").hide();
			$(".recent_info_visible[view=login]").hide();

			$("#right_recent_total_num").text(datas.total_page);
			$("#right_recent_page_num").text(datas.page);

			$(".recent_info_visible[view=is] .recent_goods_wrap dl").remove();

			var str = "";
			$(datas.product).each(function(i,pinfo){
				str += '	<dl>';
				str += '		<dt>';
				str += '			<a href="/shop/goods_view.php?id='+pinfo.id+'">';
				str += '				<img src="'+pinfo.img+'" alt="" width="85" height="85" />';
				str += '			</a>';
				str += '			<span><a href="/shop/select_option.php?id='+pinfo.id+'&mode=cart" rel="facebox"><img src="/data/daiso_data/templet/daiso/images/btns/btn_cart.gif" alt="장바구니" title="장바구니" align="absmiddle" class="cart_btn" width="" /></a></span>';
				str += '			<input type="checkbox" class="right_pid_checkbox" value="'+pinfo.id+'" validation="false" title="">';
				str += '		</dt>';
				str += '		<dd>';
				str += '			<strong>'+pinfo.price+'</strong>원';
				str += '		</dd>';
				str += '	</dl>';
			});

			$(".recent_info_visible[view=is] .recent_goods_wrap").append(str).find(".cart_btn").closest("a").facebox({
				loadingImage : '/data/daiso_data/templet/daiso/images/loading.gif',
				closeImage   : '/data/daiso_data/templet/daiso/images/close_btn01.gif'
			});

		}
	}

	function right_recent_wishlist(){
		var pid = Array();
		if($(".right_pid_checkbox:checked").length > 0){
			$(".right_pid_checkbox:checked").each(function(i){
				pid[i]=$(this).val();
			});
			right_menu_control("recent","wishlist",pid);
		}else{
			alert("선택된 상품이 없습니다.");
		}
	}

<script>
function fnSmartSearch(keyword){
	$.ajax({
		url: '/shop/new_smart_search.php',
		type: 'get',
		dataType: "html",
		data: ({mode: "smart",
				searchTerm: keyword
		}),
		success: function(result){
			if(!result){
				$('.relation_search').hide();
			}else{
				$('.relation_search').show();

				var list = JSON.parse(result);
				
				var output_view = "";
				var keywordInput = "";
				var allSearch = "";
				
				keywordInput = "<strong class=\"main_color\">"+keyword+"</strong>";
				allSearch = "<a href=\"/shop/search.php?search_text="+ keyword +"\"><img src=\"/data/daiso_data/templet/daiso/images/korea/btns/btns_total_result.gif\" alt=\"전체결과\" title=\"\" /></a>";
				if(list.product != 'N') {
					$.each(list.product, function (index, item) {	

						if(index == 0) {
							keywordInput = "<strong class=\"main_color\">"+keyword+"</strong>";
							allSearch = "<a href=\"/shop/search.php?search_text="+ keyword +"\"><img src=\"/data/daiso_data/templet/daiso/images/korea/btns/btns_total_result.gif\" alt=\"전체결과\" title=\"\" /></a>";
						}
						var img_name = item.pname;
						
						if(img_name.length > 40){
							img_name = img_name.substr(0,40) + '...';		
						}
						
						output_view +=  '			<dl>';
						output_view +=  '				<dt><img src="' + item.src + '" alt="" title="" align="absmiddle" width="58" height="58"/></dt>';
						output_view +=  '				<dd class="first">';
						output_view +=  '					<p class="color_63 oh" style="height:28px;line-height:14px;margin-bottom:10px;">';
						output_view +=  '						<a href="/shop/goods_view.php?id=' + item.id + '">' + item.pname + '</a>';
						output_view +=  '					</p>';

						if(item.sellprice == item.dcprice){
							output_view +=  '					<p class="color_2a size_11"><strong class="coor_2a">' + item.sellprice +'</strong>원</p>';
						}else{
							output_view +=  '					<p class="color_2a size_11"><span class="color_7b strike">' + item.sellprice +'</span> <strong class="coor_2a">' + item.dcprice +'</strong>원</p>';
						}

						output_view +=  '				</dd>';
						output_view +=  '				<dd class="last">';
						output_view +=  '					<div class="btn_over02" style="margin-right:2px;">';
						output_view +=  '						<a href="/shop/select_option.php?id=' + item.id + '&mode=direct" rel="facebox">';
						output_view +=  '							<img src="/data/daiso_data/templet/daiso/images/btns/low_goods1_buttom.png" alt="바로구매2">';
						output_view +=  '						</a>';
						output_view +=  '						<span><img src="/data/daiso_data/templet/daiso/images/korea/common/low_goods1_buttom_txt.png" alt="바로구매" title="" align="absmiddle"></span>';
						output_view +=  '					</div>';
						output_view +=  '					<div class="btn_over02">';
						output_view +=  '						<a href="/shop/select_option.php?id=' + item.id + '&mode=cart" rel="facebox">';
						output_view +=  '							<img src="/data/daiso_data/templet/daiso/images/btns/low_goods2_buttom.png" alt="장바구니">';
						output_view +=  '						</a>';
						output_view +=  '						<span><img src="/data/daiso_data/templet/daiso/images/korea/common/low_goods2_buttom_txt.png" alt="장바구니" title="" align="absmiddle"></span>';
						output_view +=  '					</div>';
						output_view +=  '				</dd>';
						output_view +=  '			</dl>';
						output_view +=  '			<div class="clear"></div>';
					});
				}else{
					//검색영역 숨김
					//$('.relation_search').hide();
					allSearch = "";
				}

				$('#keywordInput').html(keywordInput);
				$('#allSearch').html(allSearch);
				$('.keyword-relation-goods').html(output_view);

				setProductModal();
			}
		}
	});
}

$(function() {	
	// 체크박스 선택해제
	$( '#chkRemove' ).click( function() {
         $(".chk").removeAttr("checked");
    });
	
	$('#barCheck').click( function() {
		if($("#barCheck").is(":checked") == false){
			$(".chk").removeAttr("checked");
		}
    });
	
	var search_form=document.search_form;
	$('#search_texts').keyup(function(e) {
		var searchInputDOM = $(this),
			keyboardCode = e.keyCode;

		if (keyboardCode == 38 || keyboardCode == 40) {
			var relationSearchDOM = $('.relation_search');
			if (relationSearchDOM.is(':visible')) {
				var nextIndex = relationSearchDOM.find('.auto_area li.current').index();
				switch(keyboardCode) {
					case 38:
						nextIndex = nextIndex - 1;
						break;

					case 40:
						nextIndex = nextIndex + 1;
						break;

					default:
						break;
				}
				if (nextIndex < 0) { nextIndex = 0; }
				else if (nextIndex >= relationSearchDOM.find('.auto_area li').length) { nextIndex = 0; }

				relationSearchDOM.find('.auto_area li').removeClass('current').eq(nextIndex).addClass('current').trigger('mouseover');
			}
		}
		else if (keyboardCode == 13) {
			if ($('.relation_search .auto_area li.current').length) { 
				window.location.href = $('.relation_search .auto_area li.current').find('a').attr('href');
			}
		}
		else {
			if(searchInputDOM.val().length > 0){
				$.ajax({
					url: '/shop/new_smart_search.php',
					type: 'get',
					dataType: "html",
					data: ({
						mode: "auto",
						searchTerm: searchInputDOM.val()
					}),
					success: function(result) {
						if (!result) {
							$('.relation_search').hide();
						} else {
							$('.relation_search').show();

							var list = JSON.parse(result);
							
							var output = "";
							var output_view = "";
							var keywordInput = "";
							var allSearch = "";
							if(list.keyword != 'N') {
								$.each(list.keyword, function (index, item) {
									
									var search_text = searchInputDOM.val();
									var keyword = item.keyword; // 상품명
									
									//상품명 내 검색어 강조를 위해 치환
									keyword = keyword.replace(search_text , "<strong>" + search_text + "</strong>"); 
									if(index == 0) {
										keywordInput = "<strong class=\"main_color\">"+keyword+"</strong>";
										allSearch = "<a href=\"/shop/search.php?search_text="+ item.keyword +"\"><img src=\"/data/daiso_data/templet/daiso/images/korea/btns/btns_total_result.gif\" alt=\"전체결과\" title=\"\" /></a>";
									}

									output += '<li onmouseover="$(\'.goods_tap_wrap\').hide();$(\'.goods_tap_wrap\').eq('+ index +').show();fnSmartSearch(\''+
									item.keyword+'\')" >';
									output += '<a href="/shop/search.php?search_text=' + item.keyword + '"> ' + keyword + '';
									output += '</a>';
									//output += '<span>71</span>';
									output += '</li>';
								});
							}else {
								$('.relation_search').hide();
							}
								
							if(list.product != 'N') {
								$('.keyword-title').show();
								$.each(list.product, function (index, item) {	
									var img_name = item.pname;
									
									if(img_name.length > 40){
										img_name = img_name.substr(0,40) + '...';		
									}
									/*
									output_view +=  '<div class="goods_tap_wrap">';
									output_view +=  '<dt>';
									output_view +=  '	<a href="/shop/search.php?search_text=' + item.id+ '"><img src=' + item.src + ' alt="" title="" width="130" height="130" /></a>';
									output_view +=  '</dt>';
									output_view +=  '<dd class="size_11">';
									output_view +=  '	<p style="padding:0 0 6px 0;"><a href="/shop/search.php?search_text=' + item.id + '">'+ item.pname +'</a></p>';
									output_view +=  '	<p><strike class="color_7b">' + item.listprice +'</strike> <strong> ' + item.sellprice +'</strong>원</p>';
									output_view +=  '</dd>';
									output_view +=  '</div>';
									*/
									
									output_view +=  '			<dl>';
									output_view +=  '				<dt><img src="' + item.src + '" alt="" title="" align="absmiddle" width="58" height="58"/></dt>';
									output_view +=  '				<dd class="first">';
									output_view +=  '					<p class="color_63 oh" style="height:28px;line-height:14px;margin-bottom:10px;">';
									output_view +=  '						<a href="/shop/goods_view.php?id=' + item.id + '">' + item.pname + '</a>';
									output_view +=  '					</p>';
									if(item.sellprice == item.dcprice){
										output_view +=  '					<p class="color_2a size_11"><strong class="coor_2a">' + item.sellprice +'</strong>원</p>';
									}else{
										output_view +=  '					<p class="color_2a size_11"><span class="color_7b strike">' + item.sellprice +'</span> <strong class="coor_2a">' + item.dcprice +'</strong>원</p>';
									}
									output_view +=  '				</dd>';
									output_view +=  '				<dd class="last">';
									output_view +=  '					<div class="btn_over02" style="margin-right:2px;">';
									output_view +=  '						<a href="/shop/select_option.php?id=' + item.id + '&mode=direct" rel="facebox">';
									output_view +=  '							<img src="/data/daiso_data/templet/daiso/images/btns/low_goods1_buttom.png" alt="바로구매3">';
									output_view +=  '						</a>';
									output_view +=  '						<span><img src="/data/daiso_data/templet/daiso/images/korea/common/low_goods1_buttom_txt.png" alt="바로구매" title="" align="absmiddle"></span>';
									output_view +=  '					</div>';
									output_view +=  '					<div class="btn_over02">';
									output_view +=  '						<a href="/shop/select_option.php?id=' + item.id + '&mode=cart" rel="facebox">';
									output_view +=  '							<img src="/data/daiso_data/templet/daiso/images/btns/low_goods2_buttom.png" alt="장바구니">';
									output_view +=  '						</a>';
									output_view +=  '						<span><img src="/data/daiso_data/templet/daiso/images/korea/common/low_goods2_buttom_txt.png" alt="장바구니" title="" align="absmiddle"></span>';
									output_view +=  '					</div>';
									output_view +=  '				</dd>';
									output_view +=  '			</dl>';
									output_view +=  '			<div class="clear"></div>';
								});
							}else{
								//검색영역 숨김
								//$('.relation_search').hide();
								$('.keyword-title').hide();
								allSearch = "일치하는 키워드가 없습니다";
							}

							var category = "<dt><strong>카테고리 추천</strong></dt>";
							if(list.category != 'N') {
								$.each(list.category, function (index, item) {   	
									category += '<dd><a href="/shop/goods_list.php?cid=' + item.cid + '&depth=' + item.depth + '">'+  item.category_name +'(<strong>' + item.category_size + '</strong>개)</a></dd>';
								});
							}else{
								category += '<dd>해당하는 추천 카테고리가 없습니다</dd>';
							}

							var event_list = "<dt><strong>기획전/이벤트</strong></dt>";
							if(list.event != 'N') {
								$.each(list.event, function (index, item) {   	
									event_list += '<dd><a href="/event/goods_event.php?event_ix='+ item.event_ix +'">'+  item.event_title +'</a></dd>';
								});
							}else{
								event_list += '<dd>해당하는 기획전/이벤트가 없습니다</dd>';
							}

							$('.auto_area').html(output);
							$('#keywordInput').html(keywordInput);
							$('#allSearch').html(allSearch);
							
							//$('.keyitem').html(output_view);
							$('.keyword-relation-goods').html(output_view);
							$('.goods_tap_wrap').hide();
							$('.goods_tap_wrap').eq(0).show();
							$('.category-recommend').html(category);
							$('.event_list').html(event_list);

							setProductModal();

							var autoAreaLiDOM = $('.relation_search .auto_area li');
							autoAreaLiDOM.unbind('mouseover').bind('mouseover', function() {
								autoAreaLiDOM.removeClass('current');
								$(this).addClass('current');
							});
						}
					}
				});
			}else{
				$('.relation_search').hide();
			}
		}
	});

	$('#search-scroll-search').keyup(function(){

		if($('#search-scroll-search').val().length > 0){
			console.log('scrolsearch');
			$.ajax({
				url: '/shop/smart_search.php',
				type: 'get',
				dataType: "html",
				data: ({mode: "auto",
						searchTerm: $('#search-scroll-search').val()
				}),
				success: function(result){
					if(!result){
						$('.relation_search02').hide();

						var list = JSON.parse(result);

							$.each(list.product, function (index, item) {
		
								var search_text = $('#search_texts').val(); // 검색어
								var pname = item.pname; // 상품명
								
								if(pname.length > 20){

								}else{
									panme = pname;
								}
								//상품명 내 검색어 강조를 위해 치환
								//pname = pname.replace(search_text , "<strong>" + search_text + "</strong>"); 

								//output += '<li onmouseover="$(\'.goods_tap_wrap\').hide();$(\'.goods_tap_wrap\').eq('+ index +').show();" >';
								output += '<li>';
								output += '<a href="/shop/search.php?search_text=' + item.pname + '"> ' + pname + '';
								output += '</a>';
								output += '</li>';
								
								/*var img_name = item.pname;
								
								if(img_name.length > 40){
									img_name = img_name.substr(0,40) + '...';		
								}
								output_view +=  '<div class="goods_tap_wrap">';

								output_view +=  '</dt>';
								output_view +=  '<dd class="size_11">';
								output_view +=  '	<p style="padding:0 0 6px 0;"><a href="/shop/search.php?search_text=' + item.id + '">'+ item.pname +'</a></p>';
								output_view +=  '	<p><strike class="color_7b">' + item.listprice +'</strike> <strong> ' + item.sellprice +'</strong>원</p>';
								output_view +=  '</dd>';
								output_view +=  '</div>';*/
							});
						}else{
							//검색영역 숨김
							$('.relation_search02').hide();
						}
						
						/*var event_list = "<dt><strong>기획전/이벤트</strong></dt>";
						if(list.event != 'N') {
							$.each(list.event, function (index, item) {   	
								event_list += '<dd><a href="/event/goods_event.php?event_ix='+ item.event_ix +'">'+  item.event_title +'</a></dd>';
							});
						}else{
							event_list += '<dd>해당하는 기획전/이벤트가 없습니다</dd>';
						}*/
						$('.top_search_bar').html(output);
						
						//$('.scroll-search-promotion').html(event_list);
					}
				}

			});
		}else{
			$('.relation_search02').hide();
		}
	});
	$('.relation_search02').hide();


});

<script>
function fnSmartOnlineSearch(keyword){
	$.ajax({
		url: '/shop/new_smart_search.php',
		type: 'get',
		dataType: "html",
		data: ({mode: "smart",
				type: "online",
				searchTerm: keyword
		}),
		success: function(result){
			if(!result){
				$('.relation_search').hide();
			}else{
				$('.relation_search').show();

				var list = JSON.parse(result);
				
				var output_view = "";
				var keywordInput = "";
				var allSearch = "";
				
				keywordInput = "<strong class=\"main_color\">"+keyword+"</strong>";
				allSearch = "<a href=\"/shop/search.php?search_text="+ keyword +"\"><img src=\"/data/daiso_data/templet/daiso/images/korea/btns/btns_total_result.gif\" alt=\"전체결과\" title=\"\" /></a>";
				if(list.product != 'N') {
					$.each(list.product, function (index, item) {	

						if(index == 0) {
							keywordInput = "<strong class=\"main_color\">"+keyword+"</strong>";
							allSearch = "<a href=\"/shop/search.php?search_text="+ keyword +"\"><img src=\"/data/daiso_data/templet/daiso/images/korea/btns/btns_total_result.gif\" alt=\"전체결과\" title=\"\" /></a>";
						}
						var img_name = item.pname;
						
						if(img_name.length > 40){
							img_name = img_name.substr(0,40) + '...';		
						}
						
						output_view +=  '			<dl>';
						output_view +=  '				<dt><img src="' + item.src + '" alt="" title="" align="absmiddle" width="58" height="58"/></dt>';
						output_view +=  '				<dd class="first">';
						output_view +=  '					<p class="color_63 oh" style="height:28px;line-height:14px;margin-bottom:10px;">';
						output_view +=  '						<a href="/shop/goods_view.php?id=' + item.id + '">' + item.pname + '</a>';
						output_view +=  '					</p>';
						if(item.listprice == item.sellprice){
							output_view +=  '					<p class="color_2a size_11"><strong class="coor_2a">' + item.sellprice +'</strong>원</p>';
						}else{
							output_view +=  '					<p class="color_2a size_11"><span class="color_7b strike">' + item.listprice +'</span> <strong class="coor_2a">' + item.sellprice +'</strong>원</p>';
						}
						output_view +=  '				</dd>';
						output_view +=  '				<dd class="last">';
						output_view +=  '					<div class="btn_over02" style="margin-right:2px;">';
						output_view +=  '						<a href="/shop/select_option.php?id=' + item.id + '&mode=direct" rel="facebox">';
						output_view +=  '							<img src="/data/daiso_data/templet/daiso/images/btns/low_goods1_buttom.png" alt="바로구매4">';
						output_view +=  '						</a>';
						output_view +=  '						<span><img src="/data/daiso_data/templet/daiso/images/korea/common/low_goods1_buttom_txt.png" alt="바로구매" title="" align="absmiddle"></span>';
						output_view +=  '					</div>';
						output_view +=  '					<div class="btn_over02">';
						output_view +=  '						<a href="/shop/select_option.php?id=' + item.id + '&mode=cart" rel="facebox">';
						output_view +=  '							<img src="/data/daiso_data/templet/daiso/images/btns/low_goods2_buttom.png" alt="장바구니">';
						output_view +=  '						</a>';
						output_view +=  '						<span><img src="/data/daiso_data/templet/daiso/images/korea/common/low_goods2_buttom_txt.png" alt="장바구니" title="" align="absmiddle"></span>';
						output_view +=  '					</div>';
						output_view +=  '				</dd>';
						output_view +=  '			</dl>';
						output_view +=  '			<div class="clear"></div>';
					});
				}else{
					//검색영역 숨김
					//$('.relation_search').hide();
					allSearch = "";
				}

				$('#keywordInput').html(keywordInput);
				$('#allSearch').html(allSearch);
				$('.keyword-relation-goods').html(output_view);

				setProductModal();
			}
		}
	});
}

									output += '</a>';
									//output += '<span>12</span>';
									output += '</li>';
								});
							}
							//alert(list.product);

									*/

						setProductModal();
					}

				}

			}
		});
	
	

	});

<script>
	$(document).ready(function(){
		
		$('#search_texts2').bind('focusin',function(){
			$(this).next().css({'display':'none'});
			
		  }).bind('focusout', function(){
			var inputValue = $(this).val();
			if(inputValue == ''){
			  $(this).next().css({'display':'block'});
			}
		 });

		 $('#search_texts2').keyup(function(){
			if($('#search_texts2').val().length > 0){
				var _this = $(this);
				$.ajax({
					url: '/shop/smart_search.php',
					type: 'get',
					dataType: "html",
					data: ({mode: "auto",
							type: "lowdeal",
							searchTerm: $('#search_texts2').val()
					}),
					success: function(result){
						
						if(!result){
							_this.siblings('.relation_search02').hide(); 
						}else{
							_this.siblings('.relation_search02').show(); 
							var list = JSON.parse(result);
							//var list_cnt = list.length;
							// 변수를 선언한다.
							var output = "";
							if(list.product != 'N') {
								$.each(list.product, function (index, item) {
			
									var search_text = $('#search_texts2').val();
									var pname = item.pname;
									
									if(pname.length > 20){
										pname = pname.substr(0,20) + '...';		
									}else{
										panme = pname;
									}

									pname = pname.replace(search_text , "<strong>" + search_text + "</strong>"); 

									//console.log(pname);

									output += '<li>';
									output += '<a href="/low_deal/lowdeal_list.php?search_text=' + item.pname + '"> ' + pname + '';
									output += '</a>';
									output += '</li>';
								});
							}else{
								_this.siblings('.relation_search02').hide(); 
							}
						
							$('.low_deal_search').html(output);
						}
					}

				});
			}else{
				$(this).siblings('.relation_search02').hide(); 
			}
		});
		
	});

	function set_app(){
		$(".set_app_box").toggle();
	}
	function bookmarksite(title,url) { 
	   // Internet Explorer
	   if(document.all)
	   {
		  alert("Ctrl+D키를 누르시면 즐겨찾기에 추가하실 수 있습니다.");
	   }
	   // Google Chrome
	   else if(window.chrome){
		  alert("Ctrl+D키를 누르시면 즐겨찾기에 추가하실 수 있습니다.");
	   }
	   // Firefox
	   else if (window.sidebar) // firefox 
	   {
		   window.sidebar.addPanel(title, url, ""); 
	   }
	   // Opera
	   else if(window.opera && window.print)
	   { // opera 
		  var elem = document.createElement('a'); 
		  elem.setAttribute('href',url); 
		  elem.setAttribute('title',title); 
		  elem.setAttribute('rel','sidebar'); 
		  elem.click(); 
	   }
	} 
</script>
